<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">(All
amounts expressed in U.S. dollars unless otherwise noted)</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">AGNICO-EAGLE REPORTS 2008 RESULTS;<br>
RECORD QUARTERLY AND ANNUAL GOLD PRODUCTION;</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">RECORD GOLD RESERVES AND RESOURCES</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Toronto
(February&nbsp;18, 2009) &#150; Agnico-Eagle Mines Limited</font></b> (&#147;Agnico-Eagle&#148; or the &#147;Company&#148;)
today reported quarterly net income of $21.9 million, or $0.15 per share for
the fourth quarter of 2008.&#160; This result
includes a non-cash foreign currency translation gain of $51.5 million, or
$0.35 per share, and a tax recovery of $11.1 million, or $0.07 per share,
offset partly by a non-cash writedown of investments of $39.2 million, or $0.27
per share.&#160; In the fourth quarter of
2007, the Company reported net income of $65.2 million, or $0.46 per share.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Fourth quarter 2008 cash <i>used</i> by operating activities was $46.4 million (net of a
change in working capital of <i>minus</i> $52.1
million), down from cash <i>provided</i> by
operating activities of $48.8 million in the fourth quarter of 2007, primarily
due to lower metal prices and working capital movements, offset partly by
higher gold production.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;Compared to the fourth quarter last
year, gold production increased 48% as LaRonde continued its steady performance
and the new Goldex mine achieved its design capacity in December&#148;, said Sean
Boyd, Vice-Chairman and Chief Executive Officer.&#160; &#147;In addition, with our gold reserves at
record levels we are well positioned to continue to increase gold output with
2009 production expected to rise more than 100% from the 2008 level&#148;, added Mr.&nbsp;Boyd.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Fourth quarter 2008 highlights include:</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:left;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Record Production</font></b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> &#150; record gold production of 89,360
ounces in the fourth quarter contributing to record annual gold production of
276,762 ounces</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:left;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Good Cost Control &#150;</font></b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> operating cost per tonne targets
achieved at both LaRonde and Goldex</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:left;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Record gold reserves &#150;</font></b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> gold reserves rise 8%, or 1.4 million
ounces net of production, to 18.1 million ounces</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:left;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Record gold resources &#150;</font></b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> gold resources rise to record level,
even after conversion of 1.7 million ounces to reserves in 2008</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:left;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Gold Production Growth
Accelerating</font></b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">
&#150; Goldex achieves design capacity.&#160;
Kittila in the commissioning phase and pouring gold.&#160; Lapa and Pinos Altos on track for 2009
openings.&#160; Meadowbank set to open in
first quarter of 2010</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the full year 2008, the Company
recorded net income of $73.2 million, or $0.51 per share.&nbsp; In 2007,
Agnico-Eagle recorded net income of $139.3 million, or $1.05 per share.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Compared with 2007, full year 2008
earnings were negatively affected by a lower realized price and reduced
production of zinc.&#160; This was partially
offset by 20% higher gold production and higher realized gold prices.&#160; Full year 2008 earnings per share were also
diluted by the issuance of a total of 12.4 million shares during the year, as
previously announced.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For 2008, the Company recorded cash
provided by operating activities of $118.1 million.&nbsp;&nbsp;This is down
from 2007 when cash provided by operating activities totaled $245.5
million.&#160; The decrease in cash provided
by operating activities was largely due to the same factors that negatively
affected earnings.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company&#146;s financial position remains
strong with cash and cash equivalents of $99.4 million at December&nbsp;31,
2008 and undrawn credit lines of approximately $345 million.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Payable gold production(1)&nbsp;in the
fourth quarter of 2008 was a record 89,360 ounces at total cash costs per ounce(2)&nbsp;of
$463.&nbsp; This compares with payable gold production of 60,183 ounces, at
total cash costs per ounce of <i>minus</i>
$184 in the fourth quarter of 2007.&nbsp; The increase in total cash costs per
ounce in the fourth quarter of 2008 is mainly due to large realized and
unrealized settlement losses on zinc and copper concentrates (totaling $16
million in the fourth quarter).&#160; These
losses arose as zinc prices decreased significantly between shipment and
settlement of the concentrates in the fourth quarter.&#160; Without these settlement losses total cash
costs per ounce would have been below $300 per ounce.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Payable gold production for the full year
2008 was a record 276,762 ounces at total cash costs per ounce of $162.&#160; These costs place Agnico-Eagle&#146;s gold
production in the lowest quartile of costs in the industry.&#160; This production compares to the full year
2007 level of 230,992 ounces at total cash costs per ounce of minus $365.&#160; The higher gold production in 2008 was
largely due to the start-up of the new Goldex mine, which declared commercial
production in August.&#160; The higher costs
were largely due to the significantly lower prices, and lower production of
zinc and copper during 2008.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Conference Call Today</font></b></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
Company&#146;s senior management will host a <u>conference call on Wednesday, February&nbsp;18, 2009</u> at <b><u style="font-weight:bold;">4:30pm
(E.S.T.)</u></b> to discuss financial results and provide an
update of the Company&#146;s exploration and development activities.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Via Webcast:</font></i></b></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(1)&nbsp;Payable production of a mineral
means the quantity of mineral produced during a period contained in products
that are sold by the Company, whether such products are sold during the period
or held as inventory at the end of the period.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(2)&nbsp;Total cash costs per ounce is a
non-GAAP measure.&#160; For reconciliation of
this measure to production costs, as reported in the financial statements, see
Note 1 to the financial statements at the end of this press release.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Replay archive:</font></i></b></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Please dial the 416-640-1917 or Toll-free
access number 877-289-8525, passcode 21294130#.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
conference call will be replayed from Wednesday, February&nbsp;18, 2009</font><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> at 7</font><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">:00 PM (E.S.T.) to Wednesday, February&nbsp;25, 2009 11:59 PM (E.S.T.).</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
webcast along with presentation slides will be archived for 180 days<b><i style="font-weight:bold;">  </i></b>on the Company&#146;s website.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Cash Position Remains
Strong, Despite Large Investments in Gold Growth</font></b></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Cash and cash equivalents decreased to
$99.4 million at December&nbsp;31, 2008 from the September&nbsp;30, 2008
balance of $112.2 million.&nbsp; As expected, all of the Company&#146;s operating
cash flow and a portion of its existing cash balances were reinvested in its
gold growth projects.&nbsp;&nbsp;Capital expenditures in the quarter were
$230.5 million, including $81.3 million at Meadowbank, $7.0 million on Goldex,
$36.5 million at Kittila, $18.4 million at LaRonde, $51.4 million at Pinos
Altos and $29.5 million at Lapa. &nbsp;For the full year 2008, capital
expenditures totaled $908.9 million.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In 2009, capital expenditures are
expected to total approximately $450 million.&#160;
With its cash balances, anticipated cash flows and $345 million of
available bank lines, Agnico-Eagle is fully funded for the development and
exploration of its pipeline of gold projects in Canada, Finland and Mexico.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Gold Reserves at Record Level.&#160; New Year-End 2010 Target for Gold Reserves
Set at 20 Million to 21 Million Ounces</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">At year-end 2008, the Company&#146;s gold reserves totaled 18.1 million
ounces, an increase of 8% over 2007 levels.&#160;
The largest increase came from the Pinos Altos property where
approximately one million ounces of reserves were added in 2008.&#160; Also, the LaRonde mine replaced its produced
ounces, effectively adding a year to its mine life.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In 2009, it is expected that Agnico-Eagle&#146;s overall reserves figure
will continue to grow as the Company continues to convert its resource to
reserves and continues the exploration of its properties outside of current
resource envelopes.&#160; Agnico-Eagle&#146;s goal
is to increase gold reserves, from the existing portfolio of mines and
projects, reaching 19 million to 20 million ounces by year-end 2009.&#160; Agnico-Eagle is also presenting a target for
year-end 2010 gold reserves of between 20 million and 21 million ounces of
gold.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company anticipates that the main contributors to the targeted increase
in gold reserves, and further increases to gold resources, are likely to be:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Continued conversion of Agnico-Eagle&#146;s
current gold resources to reserves</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Depth extension of the main Suuri and
Roura zones at Kittila</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>New gold zones to the north of the
Kittila reserves</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>At Meadowbank, potential of the Goose
South zone at depth and strike extension</p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Extensions at depth at Santo Nino,
Cerro Colorado and San Eligio zones at Pinos Altos</p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>New gold zones in the Creston Mascota
area to the northwest of the Pinos Altos gold and silver reserve</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Agnico-Eagle&#146;s proven and probable byproduct reserves total
approximately 141 million ounces of silver, 584,000 tonnes of zinc and 103,000
tonnes of copper.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">See the following section titled &#147;Detailed Mineral Reserve and Resource
Data&#148; for the full details of the Company&#146;s reserve and resource position.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Tonnage amounts and contained metal amounts presented in the table and
in this news release have been rounded to the nearest thousand.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Gold Resources Rise to Record Level</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Exploration drilling during 2008 resulted in 1.7 million ounces of
resource material being converted into the reserve category.&#160; In spite of this conversion, the resources
continued to grow at several of the mines and projects.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The assumptions used in calculating the 2008 reserves and resources
were $725 per ounce gold, $13.32 per ounce silver, $1.27 per pound zinc, $3.15
per pound copper, $0.90 per pound lead, a C$/US$ exchange rate of 1.09, a
US$/Euro exchange rate of 1.37, and a Mexican Peso/US$ exchange rate of
11.00.&#160; For every 10% change in the gold
price (leaving all other assumptions unchanged), there would be an estimated 2%
change in proven and probable reserves.&#160;
The metals prices and exchange rates used in the reserve and resource
calculation are the trailing three year averages for such prices or rates in
each case, as mandated by the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The byproduct reserves and resources for silver, zinc, copper and lead
contained in the LaRonde ore body, and the silver reserves contained at Pinos
Altos, are presented in the &#147;Detailed Mineral Reserve and Resource Data&#148;
section set out below, and are not included</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">in Agnico-Eagle&#146;s gold reserve and resource totals.&#160; Please see this section for more detailed
reserve and resource estimates for all of the Company&#146;s properties.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">LaRonde Mine - Strong Production
and Cost Control Performance Continues</font></b></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The LaRonde mill processed an average of
7,025 tonnes of ore per day in the fourth quarter of 2008, compared with an
average of 7,119 tonnes per day in the corresponding period of 2007.&#160; Milling performance for the full year 2008
was 7,229 tonnes per day versus 7,325 tonnes per day in 2007.&#160; LaRonde has now been operating at a steady
state of more than 7,200 tonnes per day for more than five years, continuing to
demonstrate the reliability of this world class mine.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Minesite costs per tonne(3)&nbsp;were
approximately C$64 in the fourth quarter.&#160;
These costs are lower than the C$65 per tonne experienced in the fourth
quarter of 2007.&#160; Minesite costs per
tonne for the full year 2008 were on target at approximately C$67, only two
percent higher than 2007.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On a per ounce basis, net of byproduct
credits, LaRonde&#146;s total cash costs per ounce were $545 in the fourth quarter
on production of 54,270 ounces of gold.&#160;
This compares with the results of the fourth quarter of 2007 when total
cash costs per ounce were <i>minus</i> $184 on
production of 60,183 ounces of gold.&#160; The
increase in total cash costs is largely due to significantly lower byproduct
metal prices which caused substantial concentrate settlement losses in the
fourth quarter of 2008.&#160; This resulted in
a realized zinc price in the fourth quarter of only $0.30 per pound versus an
average spot price of $0.54 per pound.&#160;
Compared to the fourth quarter of 2007, realized zinc prices were down
71% in the fourth quarter of 2008.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the full year 2008, LaRonde&#146;s total
cash costs per ounce were $106 on gold production of 216,208 ounces, placing it
among the lowest cash cost gold mines in the industry.&#160; This compares to <i>minus</i>
$365 on gold production of 230,992 in 2007, when byproduct metals prices were
much stronger.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Gold production in 2009 at LaRonde is
expected to be approximately 203,000 ounces as the gold grade of the orebody
continues to decline (partly due to a higher gold price) until 2012 when the
deeper, gold rich, ore is accessed via the new internal shaft of the LaRonde
Extension.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">LaRonde Extension &#150; Shaft Sinking
Well Advanced</font></b></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During the fourth quarter of 2008,
approximately 163 metres of shaft sinking was completed on the new internal
shaft, compared to 137 metres during the third quarter of 2008.&#160; Shaft sinking performance has been good with
the shaft down to a depth of approximately 570 metres out of a total planned
depth of 840 metres from the underground shaft collar (which is 2,030 metres
below surface).&#160; The project remains on
schedule.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Overall,
proven and probable gold reserves at LaRonde and the LaRonde Extension total
5.0 million ounces from 35.8 million tonnes grading 4.3 grams per tonne (&#147;g/t&#148;).&#160; Life of mine</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><hr size="1" width="25%" noshade color="black" align="left"></div>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(3)&nbsp;Minesite costs per tonne is a
non-GAAP measure.&#160; For reconciliation of
this measure to production costs, as reported in the financial statements, see
Note 1 to the financial statements at the end of this news release.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">average
annual gold production is expected to be approximately 320,000 ounces per year
through 2022.&#160; First production is
expected from the new internal shaft in 2011.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Goldex Mine &#150; Achieving Targets</font></b></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Goldex mill processed an average of
6,141 tonnes per day in the fourth quarter of 2008, exceeding plan.&#160; The design capacity for the plant is
approximately 6,900 tonnes per day.&#160; This
rate has already been exceeded periodically in 2009.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During the fourth quarter of 2008,
approximately 573,000 tonnes of ore were blasted at Goldex compared with
approximately 560,000 tonnes hoisted.&#160;
For the full year 2008, approximately 1.4 million tonnes were blasted
while approximately 900,000 tonnes were hoisted.&#160; This is necessary as the mining method used
at Goldex requires some of the broken ore to be temporarily left within the
mining block as ground support.&#160; As a
result of this method, production blasting is expected to be completed in 2012,
while the anticipated mine life extends through 2017.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Minesite costs per tonne at Goldex were
approximately C$24 in the fourth quarter, down from $34 in the third quarter of
2008.&#160; As the mine started up in 2008,
there is no corresponding 2007 quarter.&#160;
Minesite costs per tonne for the full year 2008 were approximately C$27,
reflecting the start-up phase of the mine when higher costs were realized.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Fourth quarter 2008 gold production was
31,972 ounces compared with the third quarter of 2008 when gold production was
17,159 and the mine was in its initial start-up phase.&#160; The mine achieved commercial production in August&nbsp;2008.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Goldex&#146;s total cash costs per ounce were
$323 in the fourth quarter.&#160; For the full
year 2008, Goldex&#146;s total cash costs per ounce were $419 on gold production of
57,436 ounces, reflecting the partial year and the start-up phase of the
mine.&#160; Gold production for 2009 is
expected to be 165,000 ounces.&#160; Life of
mine production is expected to average 160,000 ounces annually.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A
scoping study is underway to examine the possibility of increasing the capacity
of the mine from 6,900 tonnes per day to at least 8,000 tonnes per day.&#160; This may require additions to the crushing
and grinding circuit and additions to the mining fleet.&#160; Results of the study are expected to be
released in the second quarter of 2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Kittila Mine &#150; Commercial
Production Expected in the Second Quarter of 2009</font></b></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Kittila mine poured its first gold on
January&nbsp;14, 2009.&#160; Also during the
month, the first bars were delivered to the refinery for final processing.&#160; In January, approximately 2,100 ounces of
gold were produced.&#160; As a conservative
measure, Agnico-Eagle has not budgeted any gold production in the first quarter
of 2009 while the commissioning is taking place.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The commissioning process in the mill is
proceeding in a sequential manner and is anticipated to be complete in the
second quarter of 2009.&#160; The grinding
circuit has achieved its design criteria and the autoclave is operating at
expected oxidation and throughput levels.&#160;
However, metallurgical optimization of the flotation circuit and process
optimization of the leach circuit are ongoing.&#160;
Additionally, due to the accumulation of fine</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6</font></p>

<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">ore in the bin, inadequate ore flow has
affected the operation to date.&#160; This
problem will be addressed by refining the crushing circuit.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During the fourth quarter of 2008, the
Kittila mill processed a total of 108,341 tonnes of ore resulting in 9,429
tonnes of concentrate being processed by the autoclave, and a further 3,920
tonnes of concentrate being held in the concentrate storage area at year end.&#160; At the end of the quarter, 4,590 tonnes of
concentrate was in the storage area.&#160;&#160;&#160;
Gold output in the fourth quarter was 3,118 ounces in concentrate form.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">At the end of the quarter, the ore stockpile
at Kittila contained approximately 199,000 tonnes, grading 4.8 grams per
tonne.&#160; During the quarter, mine
personnel assumed all of the mining activities including drilling, blasting and
haulage from the contractors.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Underground development exceeded plan
during the quarter achieving 859 meters on a plan of 690 meters.&#160; Many of the performance issues encountered
during the initial part of the year were resolved resulting in significantly
improved productivity.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Gold production is expected to be 125,000
ounces for the full year.&#160; Life of mine
annual production is expected to average approximately 150,000 ounces.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A
scoping study is underway examining the possibility of significantly increasing
the production rate at Kittila.&#160; This
plan involves sinking a shaft on the property.&#160;
Results of the study are expected to be released in the fourth quarter
of 2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Lapa &#150; the
Next New Gold Mine</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Good
lateral development performance was achieved in the fourth quarter with 2,375
metres being driven.&#160; An additional 1,000
metres of vertical development was also achieved.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">While
the main activity at Lapa continues to be lateral and vertical development, the
first test stope was mined during the fourth quarter of 2008.&#160; Drilling began on December&nbsp;11th on stope
80-31 and the first production blast was on December&nbsp;25th.&#160; Overall, performance of the drilling and
blasting was as expected.&#160; A total of
1,100 tonnes, grading 12.7 g/t, was mucked and placed on the surface
stockpile.&#160; The total surface stockpile
at the end of January&nbsp;2009 was approximately 31,000 tonnes grading 8.9
g/t.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
addition to the plant at LaRonde, where the Lapa ore will be processed, is
expected to be complete early in the second quarter of 2009.&#160; Lapa is expected to begin gold production
near the end of the second quarter of 2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Probable
gold reserves at Lapa total 1.1 million ounces from 3.7 million tonnes grading
8.8 grams per tonne.&#160; Life of mine
average annual gold production is expected to be approximately 115,000 ounces
per year through 2015.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Construction at Pinos Altos
Progressing as Expected</font></b></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Construction
of the new Pinos Altos mine is well advanced.&#160;
Commissioning and first gold production are expected before the end of
the third quarter of 2009.&#160; The SAG mill</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">7</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='7',FILE='C:\JMS\c900187\09-5976-1\task3371130\5976-1-ka-01.htm',USER='c900187',CD='Feb 20 06:24 2009' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">foundations
were completed and mechanical installation started.&#160; The leach pads were also completed.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During
the fourth quarter of 2008, construction advanced rapidly in the process plant,
electric line, shop/warehouse and heap leach areas.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Open
pit mining continued with 10.1 million total tonnes mined by year end,
approximately 23% above plan.&#160; First ore
was mined to the stockpile during the fourth quarter.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Underground
development productivity improved by about 12% over the previous quarter and
total development by year-end was 3,669 meters.&#160;
Performance is expected to continue to improve with the new additional
mining equipment that was delivered to the site at the beginning of 2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Pinos Altos Grows by One
Million Ounces of Gold and 27 Million Ounces of Silver</font></b></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Following
a successful drilling program in 2008, probable reserves total 3.6 million
ounces of gold and 100.0 million ounces of silver from 41.7 million tonnes
grading 2.7 grams per tonne of gold and 74.6 grams per tonne of silver.&#160; Life of mine average annual gold production
is expected to be approximately 175,000 ounces of gold and 2.6 million ounces
of silver per year over a 13 year mine life.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">However,
a feasibility study is expected to be released soon on the potential to add
incremental production from the Creston Mascota deposit, which contains 0.4
million ounces of the Pinos Altos gold reserve.&#160;
Creston Mascota is roughly 10 kilometres to the northwest of the main
Santo Nino deposit at Pinos Altos.&#160; The
study is considering a stand-alone heap leach operation.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Meadowbank
Construction Update</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Construction
of the new Meadowbank mine is well advanced.&#160;
Commissioning and first gold production are expected before the end of
the first quarter of 2010.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Probable
gold reserves total 3.6 million ounces from 32.8 million tonnes grading 3.5
grams per tonne.&#160; Life of mine average
annual gold production is expected to be approximately 350,000 ounces per year
over a 10 year mine life.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Pre-stripping
in the Portage pit is underway with approximately 800,000 tonnes of waste rock
hauled during the fourth quarter of 2008.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During
the fourth quarter of 2008, the mill, power house and service buildings were
fully enclosed. Work is currently continuing on the SAG mill foundations and
internal foundations during the winter season.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Most
of the earthwork related to the construction of the East Dike were completed by
the end of the third quarter of 2008. During the fourth quarter of 2008, the
emphasis was placed on the grouting of the foundation of the dike.&#160; Casing installation is virtually
complete.&#160; Bedrock drilling has now
progressed to 33% completion.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='8',FILE='C:\JMS\c900187\09-5976-1\task3371130\5976-1-ka-01.htm',USER='c900187',CD='Feb 20 06:24 2009' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Construction
of the Bay-Goose Dykes are scheduled for 2009 and 2010.&#160; Completion of the East Dyke will permit the
start of initial production from the Portage Open Pit while completion of the
two additional dykes will permit the extension of the Portage open pit as well
as access the higher grade ore of the Goose Island open pit by 2011.&#160; Work has started on dewatering the Portage
open pit area.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Preparations
are underway for the 2009 sea lift season. The outstanding mill and mining
equipment as well as consumables for the following year are scheduled to be
delivered this summer.&#160; It is expected to
start commissioning the plant near the beginning of 2010.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">About Agnico-Eagle</font></b></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Agnico-Eagle is a long established,
Canadian headquartered, gold producer with operations located in Quebec and
Finland, and exploration and development activities in Canada, Finland, Mexico
and the United States.&#160; Agnico-Eagle&#146;s
LaRonde mine is Canada&#146;s largest gold mine in terms of reserves.&#160; The Company has full exposure to higher gold
prices consistent with its policy of no forward gold sales.&#160; It has paid a cash dividend for 27
consecutive years.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">9</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

  <td width="1%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;border:none;border-bottom:double windowtext 2.25pt;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:1.12%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">$</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="8%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;border-bottom:double windowtext 2.25pt;border-left:none;border-right:none;border-top:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:8.88%;">
  <p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(365</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="1%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;padding:0in 0in 2.25pt 0in;width:1.0%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">)</font></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

<p style="margin:0in .2pt .0001pt 0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in .2pt .0001pt 0in;"><hr size="1" width="25%" noshade color="black" align="left"></div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Notes:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .2pt .0001pt 0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(1)&nbsp;Total cash costs per ounce, net of copper, zinc and byproduct
credits. Total is weighted average based on commercial production ounces.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .3in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(2)&nbsp;Includes non-commercial production of 10,089 ounces in full
year.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .2pt .0001pt 0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(3)&nbsp;Includes non-commercial production of 3,118 ounces in Q4 and in
full year.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">AGNICO-EAGLE MINES LIMITED</font></b></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="1" width="25%" noshade color="black" align="left"></div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Notes:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(i)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Under the Company&#146;s revenue recognition
policy, revenue is recognized on concentrates when legal title passes. Since
total cash costs are calculated on a production basis, this inventory
adjustment reflects the sales margin on the portion of concentrate production
for which revenue has not been recognized in the&nbsp;period.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(ii)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Total cash costs is not a recognized measure
under US GAAP and this data may not be comparable to data presented by other
gold producers. The Company believes that this generally accepted industry
measure is a realistic indication of operating performance and is useful in
allowing year over year comparisons. As illustrated in the table above, this
measure is calculated by adjusting Production Costs as shown in the Consolidated
Statements of Income and Comprehensive Income for net byproduct revenues,
royalties, inventory adjustments and asset retirement provisions. This measure
is intended to provide investors with information about the cash generating
capabilities of the Company&#146;s mining operations. Management uses this measure
to monitor the performance of the Company&#146;s mining operations. Since market
prices for gold are quoted on a per ounce basis, using this per ounce measure
allows management to assess the mine&#146;s cash generating capabilities at various
gold prices. Management is aware that this per ounce measure of performance can
be impacted by fluctuations in byproduct metal prices and exchange rates.
Management compensates for the limitation inherent with this measure by using
it in conjunction with the minesite costs per tonne measure (discussed below)
as well as other data prepared in accordance with US GAAP. Management also
performs sensitivity analyses in order to quantify the effects of fluctuating
metal prices and exchange&nbsp;rates.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(iii)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>This inventory adjustment reflects production
costs associated with unsold concentrates.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(iv)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Minesite costs per tonne is not a recognized
measure under US GAAP and this data may not be comparable to data presented by
other gold producers. As illustrated in the table above, this measure is
calculated by adjusting Production Costs as shown in the Consolidated
Statements of Income and Comprehensive Income for inventory and asset
retirement provisions and then dividing by tonnes processed through the mill.
Since total cash costs data can be affected by fluctuations in byproduct metal
prices and exchange rates, management believes minesite costs per tonne
provides additional information regarding the performance of mining operations
and allows management to monitor operating costs on a more consistent basis as
the per tonne measure eliminates the cost variability associated with varying
production levels. Management also uses this measure to determine the economic
viability of mining blocks. As each mining block is evaluated based on the net
realizable value of each tonne mined, in order to be economically viable the
estimated revenue on a per tonne basis must be in excess of the minesite costs
per tonne. Management is aware that this per tonne measure is impacted by
fluctuations in production levels and thus uses this evaluation tool in
conjunction with production costs prepared in accordance with US GAAP. This
measure supplements production cost information prepared in accordance with US
GAAP and allows investors to distinguish between changes in production costs
resulting from changes in production versus changes in operating performance.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">15</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Forward-Looking
Statements</font></b></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
information in this press release has been prepared as at February&nbsp;18,
2008. Certain statements contained in this press release constitute &#147;forward-looking
statements&#148; within the meaning of the United States Private Securities
Litigation Reform Act of 1995 and forward looking information under the
provisions of Canadian provincial securities laws. When used in this document,
words such as &#147;anticipate&#148;, &#147;expect&#148;, &#147;estimate,&#148; &#147;forecast,&#148; &#147;planned&#148;, &#147;wil</font><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">l&#148;, &#147;likely&#148; and similar expressions are
intended to identify forward-looking statements and are referred to herein as &#147;forward-looking
statements&#148;.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Such statements include without
limitation: the Company&#146;s forward looking production guidance, including
estimated ore grades, metal production, life of mine horizons, and projected
exploration and capital expenditures, including costs and other estimates upon
which such projections are based; the Company&#146;s goal to increase its mineral
reserves and resources; and other statements and information regarding
anticipated trends with respect to the Company&#146;s operations and exploration.
Such statements reflect the Company&#146;s views as at the date of this press
release and are subject to certain risks, uncertainties and assumptions.
Forward-looking statements are necessarily based upon a number of factors and
assumptions that, while considered reasonable by Agnico-Eagle as of the date of
such statements, are inherently subject to significant business, economic and
competitive uncertainties and contingencies. The factors and assumptions of
Agnico-Eagle contained in this news release, which may prove to be incorrect,
include, but are not limited to, the assumptions set forth herein and in
management&#146;s discussion and analysis as well as: that there are no significant
disruptions affecting operations, whether due to labour disruptions, supply
disruptions, damage to equipment, natural occurrences, political changes, title
issues or otherwise; that permitting, development and expansion at each of
Agnico-Eagle&#146;s development projects proceeds on a basis consistent with current
expectations, and that Agnico-Eagle does not change its development plans
relating to such projects; that the exchange rate between the Canadian dollar,
European Union euro, Mexican peso and the United&#160; States dollar will be approximately
consistent with current levels or as set out in this news release; prices for
gold, silver, zinc, copper and lead will be consistent with Agnico-Eagle&#146;s
expectations; that prices for key mining and construction supplies, including
labour costs, remain consistent with Agnico-Eagle&#146;s current expectations; that
production meets expectations; that Agnico-Eagle&#146;s current estimates of mineral
reserves, mineral resources, mineral grades and mineral recovery are accurate;
that there are no material delays in the timing for completion of ongoing
development projects; and that there are no material variations in the current
tax and regulatory environment.&#160; Many
factors, known and unknown, could cause the actual results to be materially
different from those expressed or implied by such forward looking statements.
Such risks include, but are not limited to: the volatility of prices of gold
and other metals; uncertainty of mineral reserves, mineral resources, mineral
grades and mineral recovery estimates; uncertainty of future production,
capital expenditures, and other costs; currency fluctuations; financing of
additional capital requirements; cost of exploration and development programs;
mining risks; risks associated with foreign operations; governmental and
environmental regulation; the volatility of the Company&#146;s stock price; and
risks associated with the Company&#146;s byproduct metal derivative strategies. For
a more detailed discussion of such risks and other factors, see the Company&#146;s
Annual Information Form&nbsp;and Annual Report on Form&nbsp;20-F for the year
ended December&nbsp;31, 2007, as well as the Company&#146;s other filings with the
Canadian Securities Administrators and the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission
(the &#147;SEC&#148;). The Company does not intend, and does not assume any obligation,
to update these forward-looking statements and information, except as required
by law. Accordingly, readers are advised not to place undue reliance on
forward-looking statements. Certain of the foregoing</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">17</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">statements, primarily related to
projects, are based on preliminary views of the Company with respect to, among
other things, grade, tonnage, processing, mining methods, capital costs, total
cash costs, minesite costs, and location of surface infrastructure and actual
results and final decisions may be materially different from those current
anticipated.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Notes To Investors
Regarding The Use Of Resources</font></b></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Cautionary Note To Investors
Concerning Estimates Of Measured And Indicated Resources.</font></b></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This press
release may use the terms &#147;measured resources&#148; and &#147;indicated resources&#148;. We
advise investors that while those terms are recognized and required by Canadian
regulations, the SEC does not recognize them. <b>Investors
are cautioned not to assume that any part or all of mineral deposits in these
categories will ever be converted into reserves</b>.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Cautionary Note To
Investors Concerning Estimates Of Inferred Resources.</font></b></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This press
release may also use the term &#147;inferred resources&#148;. We advise investors that
while this term is recognized and required by Canadian regulations, the SEC
does not recognize it. &#147;Inferred resources&#148; have a great amount of uncertainty
as to their existence, and great uncertainty as to their economic and legal
feasibility. It cannot be assumed that all or any part of an inferred mineral
resource will ever be upgraded to a higher category. Under Canadian rules,
estimates of inferred mineral resources may not form the basis of feasibility
or pre-feasibility studies, except in rare cases. <b>Investors are cautioned not to assume that part or all of an inferred
resource exists, or is economically or legally mineable.</b></font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Scientific And Technical
Data</font></b></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Agnico-Eagle
Mines Limited is reporting mineral resource and reserve estimates in accordance
with the CIM guidelines for the estimation, classification and reporting of
resources and reserves.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Cautionary Note To U.S.
Investors</font></b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">  <b>-</b> The
SEC permits U.S. mining companies, in their filings with the SEC, to disclose
only those mineral deposits that a company can economically and legally extract
or produce. We use certain terms in this press release, such as &#147;measured&#148;, &#147;indicated&#148;,
and &#147;inferred&#148;, and &#147;resources&#148; that the SEC guidelines strictly prohibit U.S.
registered companies from including in their filings with the SEC. U.S.
Investors are urged to consider closely the disclosure in our Form&nbsp;20-F,
which may be obtained from us, or from the SEC&#146;s website at: </font><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">http://sec.gov/edgar.shtml. &#160;A &#147;final&#148;
or &#147;bankable&#148; feasibility study is required to meet the requirements to
designate reserves under Industry Guide 7.&#160;
Estimates were calculated using historic three-year average metals
prices and foreign exchange rates in accordance with the SEC Industry Guide
7.&#160; Industry Guide 7 requires the use of
prices that reflect current economic conditions at the time of reserve
determination which Staff of the SEC has interpreted to mean historic
three-year average prices.&#160; The
assumptions used for the mineral reserves and resources estimate reported by
the Company on February&nbsp;18th, 2009 were based on three year&#160; average prices for the period ending December&nbsp;31,
2008&#160; of $725 per ounce&#160; gold, $13.32 per ounce silver, $1.27 per
pound zinc, $3.15 per pound copper, $0.90 per pound lead and C$/US$, US$/Euro
and MXP/US$ exchange rates of 1.09, 1.37 and 11.00, respectively.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">18</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>
